{: .only-website }
  *This is a work in progress jointly with Marc Bezem. Some of
  the following proofs are collapsed or hidden to reduce the size of the document.
  Nevertheless, the reader can click on them to open the full description.
  Pictures are also clickable.*

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: .equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

Using the flattening lemma we can prove this equivalence:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<a id="1220" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="1225" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="1232" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>
<a id="1253" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="1260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">_</a> <a id="1262" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  `S¹` type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point and one no trivial path
called *path* as we can see in the following picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png){: width="%30" }
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

Induction principle on paths:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2723" class="Comment">-- Postulate.</a>
  <a id="2739" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

## `pS` type

The `pS` type as the figure below shows, it is a circle with two edges
in opposite direction between two points. Notice this HIT is just different
form the suspension of booleans (Σ 2) by reversing one arrow.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png){: width="%40" }
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## `S¹ ≃ pS`

**Lemma 1** . $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**. We proceed as usual. Defining the outgoing functions and proving
the homotopies. We prove the equivalence by quasiinverse equivalence.

For this equivalence, we need to find a proper candidate to correspond
with the `loop` path of `S¹`. Our propose is `p₀₀`, the path `p₀₁ · p₁₀`.
This choice makes sense because
`p₀₀` suggests a loop, closing the circuit with the arrows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="p₀₀"></a><a id="5972" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5972" class="Function">p₀₀</a> <a id="5976" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a> <a id="5982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6009" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="5985" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a>
<a id="5989" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5972" class="Function">p₀₀</a> <a id="5993" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5995" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3573" class="Postulate">p₀₁</a> <a id="5999" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7119" class="Function Operator">·</a> <a id="6001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Postulate">p₁₀</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

#### Outgoing functions

We define the function `f` that goes from `S¹` to `pS` type.
Which it means we need to use the recursion principle of the circle.
We map `base` to `pS₀` and the action on `loop` to
`(tr (λ p → pS₀ == pS₀) loop p₀₀)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6273" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Lemma₁"></a><a id="6280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6280" class="Module">Lemma₁</a> <a id="6287" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="6296" class="Keyword">private</a>
    <a id="Lemma₁.f"></a><a id="6308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="6310" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="6315" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3470" class="Function">pS</a>
    <a id="6324" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="6326" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2048" class="Function">S¹-rec</a> <a id="6335" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3470" class="Function">pS</a> <a id="6338" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a> <a id="6342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#15767" class="Function">tr</a> <a id="6346" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="6349" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6349" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="6351" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a> <a id="6357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6009" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="6360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a><a id="6363" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1775" class="Postulate">loop</a> <a id="6370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5972" class="Function">p₀₀</a><a id="6373" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

For the inverse function of `f` we have `g` which goes from `pS` to `S¹`. `g` is
defined by the recursion principle of `pS` type. The correspondence in this case
maps all the points to `base` in S¹, and the arrows `p₀₁` and `p₁₀` to `loop ²`
and `loop ⁻¹` respectively. The reason for these last choices is because their
concatenation gives a `loop` which is exactly the correspondence that we want to
have. Another possible choices would be if we take instead `loop` and `refl
base` but that would give us a different proof and `p₀₀` could be something
else.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6963" class="Comment">-- Inverse</a>
    <a id="Lemma₁.g"></a><a id="6978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6978" class="Function">g</a> <a id="6980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3470" class="Function">pS</a> <a id="6985" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a>
    <a id="6994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6978" class="Function">g</a> <a id="6996" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3705" class="Function">pS-rec</a> <a id="7005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="7008" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a> <a id="7013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a> <a id="7018" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1775" class="Postulate">loop</a> <a id="7024" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1864" class="Function Operator">²</a><a id="7025" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7027" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1775" class="Postulate">loop</a> <a id="7033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7495" class="Function Operator">⁻¹</a><a id="7035" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, let's prove the respective homotopies to show the equivalence.

####  `f ∘ g ~ id`

To prove the homotopy $$f ∘ g \sim \mathsf{id}$$, we also need recursion
principle of `pS` type as it follows.

- Case `pS₁`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7280" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.q₁"></a><a id="7290" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#7290" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="7293" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7295" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="7297" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6978" class="Function">g</a> <a id="7300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3527" class="Function">pS₁</a><a id="7303" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7305" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6009" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="7308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3527" class="Function">pS₁</a>
  <a id="7314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#7290" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="7317" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7519" class="Function Operator">!</a> <a id="7321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5972" class="Function">p₀₀</a> <a id="7325" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7119" class="Function Operator">·</a> <a id="7327" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7519" class="Function Operator">!</a> <a id="7329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5972" class="Function">p₀₀</a> <a id="7333" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#7119" class="Function Operator">·</a> <a id="7335" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3573" class="Postulate">p₀₁</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

      <a id="10482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6189" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="10487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a>

Finally, by path induction on `pS` type, we got the homotopy.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10587" class="Comment">-- Homotopy.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₁"></a><a id="10602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#10602" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="10605" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10607" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="10609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4135" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="10611" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6978" class="Function">g</a> <a id="10613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#28764" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="10615" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="10620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#10602" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="10623" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#4530" class="Function">pS-ind</a> <a id="10632" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="10634" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10635" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6189" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="10640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a><a id="10643" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#7290" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="10648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#7417" class="Function">dpath₀</a> <a id="10655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#8883" class="Function">dpath₁</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

####  g ∘ f ~ id

To prove the homotopy $$g ∘ f \sim \mathsf{id}$$, we proceed by induction on
the circle. For the `base` case, `refl base` works since `g (f base)` is
definitionally equal to `base`.


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10891" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₂-base"></a><a id="10901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#10901" class="Function">H₂-base</a> <a id="10909" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6978" class="Function">g</a> <a id="10913" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="10916" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a><a id="10920" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6009" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="10925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12822" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₂"></a><a id="12836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12836" class="Function">H₂</a> <a id="12839" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12841" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6978" class="Function">g</a> <a id="12843" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4135" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="12845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6308" class="Function">f</a> <a id="12847" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#28764" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="12849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="12854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12836" class="Function">H₂</a> <a id="12857" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2503" class="Function">S¹-ind</a> <a id="12866" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="12868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#10901" class="Function">H₂-base</a> <a id="12876" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#11038" class="Function">H₂-loop</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, everything we needed to prove the equivalence is
and the equivalence is by quasiinverse equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13018" class="Comment">-- Equivalence.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.S¹-≃-pS"></a><a id="13036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13036" class="Function">S¹-≃-pS</a> <a id="13044" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="13049" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#33341" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="13051" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3470" class="Function">pS</a>

## Action on paths of pairs

For the following equivalence, `Σ S¹ P ≃ pS`, we need first to
understand how is the action on paths of pairs, which appears as Lemma
6.12.7 in {% cite hottbook %}.

In context:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13322" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Lemma₂"></a><a id="13329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13329" class="Module">Lemma₂</a> <a id="13336" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="13338" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13343" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13343" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13345" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13347" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#973" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="13352" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="13353" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13357" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13358" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13360" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13362" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13343" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13364" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13366" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#973" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="13371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="13372" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13376" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Bound">Z</a> <a id="13379" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#973" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="13386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13337" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="13387" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13391" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13392" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13392" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="13394" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13396" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13397" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13397" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13399" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13343" class="Bound">A</a><a id="13402" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13404" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13358" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13408" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13397" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13410" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Bound">Z</a><a id="13413" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13415" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The function `f` is curried version of the function `d`,
we made its definition private since it can interfere with other
definitions of the same symbol `f`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13605" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="13615" class="Keyword">private</a>
    <a id="Lemma₂.f"></a><a id="13627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13627" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13629" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#2182" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="13633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13343" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13635" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="13638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13638" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13640" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13358" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13644" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13638" class="Bound">a</a><a id="13645" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13647" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Bound">Z</a>
    <a id="13655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13627" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13657" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13658" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="13660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#2260" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13662" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13663" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13665" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13667" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13392" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="13670" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13658" class="Bound">a</a><a id="13671" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13662" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

What we want to prove is that action on pairs is identified with a no trivial
composition as it follows. Once we do path induction on `α` we have `a₂ = a₁`
and ‵α = idp`. We proceed doing path induction on the pathover `γ` which is now
a path in the same fiber `C c₁` transporting along the reflexivity path and
`c₁ = c₂`, `γ = idp`. All this gives us trivial paths in the composition.
Therefore, we inhabit the lemma with a proof of reflexivity.

<a id="15189" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15194" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13329" class="Module">Lemma₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## `Σ S¹ P ≃ pS`

**Lemma 3.** $$ \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS $$ where
$$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

`P` is a type family defined by the recursion principle of the circle.
When it is the `base` case, `P base` is definitionally equal to the booleans `Bool`,
and when `P` is acting on `loop`, we must have a path `Bool == Bool`, which is
possible by Univalence Axiom and the equivalence `neg`, the negation of a boolean.
Let's define this type family formally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15732" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Lemma₃"></a><a id="15739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15739" class="Module">Lemma₃</a> <a id="15746" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="15753" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
<a id="neg"></a><a id="15761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15761" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="15765" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3086" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="15772" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3086" class="Datatype">Bool</a>

  <a id="15882" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="15892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15892" class="Function">h</a> <a id="15894" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15761" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="15900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4135" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="15902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15761" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="15906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#28764" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a>
    <a id="15915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15892" class="Function">h</a> <a id="15917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3107" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a>  <a id="15923" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6063" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>
    <a id="15933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15892" class="Function">h</a> <a id="15935" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3122" class="InductiveConstructor">false</a> <a id="15941" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6063" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The type family `P : S¹ → Type₀`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="P"></a><a id="16007" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#16007" class="Function">P</a> <a id="16009" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="16014" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1023" class="Function">Type₀</a>
<a id="16022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#16007" class="Function">P</a> <a id="16024" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16026" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2048" class="Function">S¹-rec</a> <a id="16033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1023" class="Function">Type₀</a> <a id="16039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3086" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="16044" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16045" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#53341" class="Function">ua</a> <a id="16048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#15825" class="Function">neg-eq</a><a id="16054" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

**Proof.** We proceed as usual to show the equivalence.
We define the outgoing functions `f : Σ S¹ P → pS`, `g : pS → Σ S¹ P`
and the homotopies `f ∘ g ~ id` and `g ∘ f ∼ id`. Let's start defining
the function `f`.

### `f : Σ S¹ P → pS`

{: .foldable until="11" }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="f"></a><a id="16346" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#16346" class="Function">f</a> <a id="16348" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="16351" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#2182" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="16353" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="16356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#16007" class="Function">P</a> <a id="16358" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16360" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3470" class="Function">pS</a>

### `g ∘ f ∼ id`

Taking inspiration from Flattening lemma's proof in Section 6
in {% cite hottbook %}, we got the following proof.

Finally, the equivalence:
